select  distinct z.numfactu, b.fechafac,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechafac as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) 
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento)
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) descuento,

 (
 select  (sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) -sum(descuento))
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) total

 from cma_DFactura z
 inner join cma_MFactura b On z.numfactu=b.numfactu  
 inner join MInventario c On c.coditems=z.coditems
 inner join MClientes d On d.codclien=b.codclien   
 where b.fechafac between   '07/01/2019' and '08/31/2019'  and b.statfact=3  AND b.codmedico='333' and z.coditems  not in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ,'0000000000')

union all

  select  distinct z.numnotcre, b.fechanot,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechanot as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre 
 ) descuento,

 (
 select  (sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) -sum(descuento)) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre
 ) total

 from CMA_Dnotacredito z
 inner join CMA_Mnotacredito b On z.numnotcre=b.numnotcre
 inner join MInventario c On c.coditems=z.coditems
 inner join MClientes d On d.codclien=b.codclien   
 where b.fechanot between  '07/01/2019' and '08/31/2019'  and b.statnc=3  AND b.codmedico='333' and z.coditems  not in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ,'0000000000')
 order by numfactu desc

select  distinct z.numfactu, b.fechafac,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechafac as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) 
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento)
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) descuento,

 (
 select  (sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) -sum(descuento))
 from cma_DFactura a 
 where z.numfactu=a.numfactu
 ) total

 from cma_DFactura z
 inner join cma_MFactura b On z.numfactu=b.numfactu  
 inner join MInventario c On c.coditems=z.coditems
 inner join MClientes d On d.codclien=b.codclien   
 where b.fechafac between   '07/01/2019' and '07/31/2019'  and b.statfact=3  AND b.codmedico='333' and z.coditems  not in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ,'0000000000')

union all

  select  distinct z.numnotcre, b.fechanot,convert(varchar(10), cast(b.fechanot as date), 101) fecha,nombres,
 (
 select  sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre
 ) subtotal,
 (
 select  sum(descuento) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre 
 ) descuento,

 (
 select  (sum(a.cantidad*a.precunit) -sum(descuento)) *-1
 from CMA_Dnotacredito a 
 where z.numnotcre=a.numnotcre
 ) total

 from CMA_Dnotacredito z
 inner join CMA_Mnotacredito b On z.numnotcre=b.numnotcre
 inner join MInventario c On c.coditems=z.coditems
 inner join MClientes d On d.codclien=b.codclien   
 where b.fechanot between  '07/01/2019' and '07/31/2019'  and b.statnc=3  AND b.codmedico='333' and z.coditems  not in ( 'CMKCINTRON','CMKCINT1CO','CMKCINTSEG' ,'0000000000')
 order by numfactu desc
